var site_device = 'web';
var dfp_device = 'desktop';
if (window.screen.width < 480) {
    site_device = 'mobile';
    dfp_device = 'mobile';
} else if (window.screen.width<990 || /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
    dfp_device = 'tablet';
}

function getDFPTag(url) {
    var tag = url.replace('[DEVICE]', dfp_device);
    try{
        var nugg = wads.public.getCustomParamsNuggForDFP();
        tag += encodeURIComponent(nugg?'&'+nugg:'');
    }catch(e){}
    return tag;
}

function wadsBeforeStart() {
    wads.callBaseUrlAutopromo    = 'http://autopromotion.purepeople.com';
    wads.cookieBaseUrlAutopromo  = 'http://autopromotion.purepeople.com';
    wads.callBaseUrlAcceptable   = 'http://acceptable.purepeople.com';
    wads.cookieBaseUrlAcceptable = 'http://acceptable.purepeople.com';
    if (window.screen.width<480) {
        wads.sitepage = wads.sitepage.replace('_web/', '_mobile/');
    } else if(window.screen.width<990 || /Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
        wads.sitepage = wads.sitepage.replace('_web/', '_tablet/');
    }
}

	window.WB_mobile_detection = (function(){

		// usage : 
		// WB_mobile_detection.isMobile() => true|false
		// WB_mobile_detection.isMobile("iphone") => true|false
		function isMobile(type) {

			var ua = navigator.userAgent;

			var isAndroid 	 = !!ua.match(/Android/i),
				isBlackBerry = !!ua.match(/BlackBerry/i),
				isIphone 	 = !!ua.match(/iPhone/i),
				isIpad 	     = !!ua.match(/iPad/i),
				isIpod 		 = !!ua.match(/iPod/i),
				isIos 		 = isIphone || isIpad,
				isOpera 	 = !!ua.match(/Opera Mini/i),
				isWindows 	 = !!ua.match(/IEMobile/i)
			;

			switch (type){

				case "android":    return isAndroid;
				case "blackBerry": return isBlackBerry;
				case "iphone": 	   return isIphone;
				case "ipad": 	   return isIpad;
				case "ipod": 	   return isIpod;
				case "ios": 	   return isIos;
				case "opera":      return isOpera;
				case "windows":    return isWindows;
				default: 		   return isAndroid || isBlackBerry || isIphone || isIpad || isIpod || isOpera || isWindows;
			}
		}

		function createCookie (name,value,days) {
			if (days) {
				var date = new Date();
				date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
				var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
			}
			else var expires = "";
			document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
		}

		function readCookie (name) {
			var nameEQ = name + "=";
			var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
			for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
				var c = ca[i];
				while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
				if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
			}
			return null;
		}
		function eraseCookie (name) {
			createCookie(name,"",-1);
		}

		// Module API
		return {
			isMobile     : isMobile,
			createCookie : createCookie,
			readCookie   : readCookie,
			eraseCookie  : eraseCookie,
			storesUrls: {

            tracker.addTrigger('disqus', 'Disqus');

        WB.defer(function() {
            // if country code is in cookie, send whithout json request
            if(WB.utils.get_cookie('country_code')) {
                var country_code = WB.utils.get_cookie('country_code')
                data_layer['visitor_country'] = country_code;
                tracker.send(data_layer, ["gtm"]);
            }else{
                $j.getJSON("/default/ajax-geoloc/get-infos-internet-user", function (data) {
                    if (data.error) {
                        // if there is an error returned then send with empty value
                        data_layer['visitor_country'] = '';
                        tracker.send(data_layer, ["gtm"]);
                        return;
                    }
                    // if json returnd is ok, send data_layer with country code
                    data_layer['visitor_country'] = data.country_code;
                    tracker.send(data_layer, ["gtm"]);
                    WB.utils.set_cookie('country_code', data.country_code, 1, '/');
                });
            }
        });
